size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）与审计相关的控制；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）对相关控制了解的性质和程度；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）内部控制的要素。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（一）内部控制的一般性质和特征<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-width: 95%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">内部控制的目标</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>52</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">．设计、执行和维护内部控制，目的是应对识别出的对被审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">单位实现下列目标产生不利影响的经营风险：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）财务报告的可靠性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）经营的效果和效率；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）遵守适用的法律法规。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">内部控制设计、执行和维护的方式因被审计单位的规模与复杂程</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">度的不同而不同。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>53</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．小型被审计单位可能采用非正式和简单的流程和程序实现内</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">部控制的目标。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">内部控制的固有限制</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>54</SPAN>．内部控制无论如何有效，都只能为被审计单位实现财务报告<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">目标提供合理保证。内部控制实现目标的可能性受其固有限制的影</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">响。这些限制包括在决策时人为判断可能出现错误和因人为失误而导</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">致内部控制失效。例如，控制的设计和修改可能存在失误。同样地，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">控制的运行可能无效，例如，由于负责复核信息的人员不了解复核的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">目的或没有采取适当的措施，内部控制生成的信息</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（如例外报告</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt">）</SPAN>没<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">有得到有效使用。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>55</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．控制可能由于两个或更多的人员串通或管理层不当地凌驾于</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">内部控制之上而被规避。例如，管理层可能与客户签订</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>背后协议</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">修改标准的销售合同条款和条件，从而导致不适当的收入确认。再如，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">软件中的编辑控制旨在识别和报告超过赊销信用额度的交易，但这一</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">控制可能被凌驾或不能得到执行。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>56</SPAN>．在设计和执行控制时，管理层可能会对选择执行的控制的性<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">质和范围以及选择承担的风险的性质和程度作出判断。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>57</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．小型被审计单位拥有的员工通常较少，限制了其职责分离的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">程度。但是，在业主管理的小型被审计单位，业主兼经理可以实施比</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">大型被审计单位更有效的监督。这种监督可以弥补职责分离有限的局</SPAN>限性。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>58</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">．另一方面，由于内部控制系统较为简单，业主兼经理更有可</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">能凌驾于控制之上。注册会计师在识别由于舞弊导致的重大错报风险</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">时需要考虑这一问题。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">对内部控制要素的划分</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>59</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．审计准则将内部控制划分为以下五个要素，为注册会计师考</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">虑内部控制的不同方面如何影响审计提供有用的框架：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）控制环境；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）风险评估过程；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）与财务报告相关的信息系统（包括相关业务流程）与沟通；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）控制活动；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）对控制的监督。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.4pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">被审计单位并不一定按照这种划分方法设计、执行和维护内部控</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">制以及划分特定要素。注册会计师也可以使用不同于本准则方法的术</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">语或框架说明内部控制的不同方面及其对审计的影响，只要能够涵盖</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">本准则所述的所有要素。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>60</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">．由于内部控制五项要素与财务报表审计相关，本指南第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>77</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">段至第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>121</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">段对其进行了说明。本指南附录</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">进一步解释了这些内部控制要素。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>与注册会计师风险评估相关的内部控制的人工和自动化成分的<SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">特征</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>61</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．被审计单位的内部控制系统包含人工成分，通常也包含自动</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">化成分。人工或自动化成分的特征，与注册会计师的风险评估以及在</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">此基础上实施的进一步审计程序相关。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.95pt">．内部控制中采用的人工成分和自动化成分，将影响交易生成、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">记录、处理和报告的方式。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）人工系统的控制可能包括对交易的批准和复核，编制调节表并对调节项目进行跟进。被审计单位也可能采用自动化程序生成、记录、处理和报告交易，在这种情况下以电子文档取代纸质文件。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）信息技术系统中的控制是自动化控制（如嵌入计算机程序的控制<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">和人工控制的组合。人工控制可能独立于信息技术，可能利</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">用信息技术生成的信息，或可能只限用于监督信息技术和自动化控制</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">的有效运行或者处理例外事项。如果采用信息技术生成、记录、处理和报告交易和财务报表中包含的其他财务数据，系统和程序可能包括</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">与财务报表重大账户认定相关的控制，或可能对依赖于信息技术的人</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">工控制的有效运行非常关键。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.4pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">内部控制中人工成分和自动化成分的组合，因被审计单位使用信</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">息技术的性质和复杂程度而异。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>63</SPAN>．一般而言，信息技术对被审计单位内部控制的作用在于使被<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">审计单位能够：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）在处理大量的交易或数据时，一贯运用事先确定的业务规则，并进行复杂运算；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）提高信息的及时性、可获得性及准确性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）促进对信息的深入分析；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）提高对被审计单位的经营业绩及其政策和程序执行情况进行监督的能力；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）降低控制被规避的风险；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>）通过对应用程序系统、数据库系统和操作系统执行安全控制，提高不兼容职务分离的有效性。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>64</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．信息技术也可能对被审计单位内部控制产生特定风险，这些</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">风险包括：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）所依赖的系统或程序不能正确处理数据，或处理了不正确的数据，或两种情况并存；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）未经授权访问数据，可能导致数据的毁损或对数据不恰当<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.95pt">的修改，包括记录未经授权或不存在的交易，或不正确地记录了交易。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">多个用户同时访问同一数据库可能会造成特定风险；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）信息技术人员可能获得超越其职责范围的数据访问权限，因此破坏了系统应有的职责分工；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）未经授权改变主文档的数据；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）未经授权改变系统或程序；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>）未能对系统或程序作出必要的修改；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN>）不恰当的人为干预；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>）可能丢失数据或不能访问所需要的数据。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>65</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．在处理下列需要主观判断或酌情处理的情形时，内部控制的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">人工成分可能更为适当：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）存在大额、异常或偶发的交易；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）存在难以界定、预计或预测的错误的情况；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）针对变化的情况，需要对现有的自动化控制进行人工干预；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）监督自动化控制的有效性。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>66</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．内部控制中的人工成分可能比自动化成分的可靠性低，原因</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">是人工成分可能更容易被规避、忽视或凌驾，以及更容易产生简单错</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">误和失误。因此，不能假定人工控制能够一贯运用。人工控制在下列</SPAN>情形中可能是不适当的：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）存在大量或重复发生的交易，或者事先可预计或预测的错误能够通过自动化控制参数得以防止或发现并纠正；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）用特定方法实施控制的控制活动可得到适当设计和自动化处理。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>67</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．内部控制风险的程度和性质取决于被审计单位信息系统的性</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">质和特征。考虑到信息系统的特征，被审计单位可以通过建立有效的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">控制，应对由于采用信息技术或人工成分而产生的风险。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体>（二）与审计相关的控制<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>68</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．被审计单位的目标与为实现目标提供合理保证的控制之间存</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">在直接关系。被审计单位的目标和控制，与财务报告、经营及合规有</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">关。但这些目标和控制并非都与注册会计师的风险评估相关。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>69</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．注册会计师在判断一项控制单独或连同其他控制是否与审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">相关时可能考虑下列事项：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）重要性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）相关风险的重要程度；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）被审计单位的规模；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）被审计单位业务的性质，包括组织结构和所有权特征；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）被审计单位经营的多样性和复杂性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>）适用的法律法规；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN>）内部控制的情况和适用的要素；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>）作为内部控制组成部分的系统（包括使用服务机构）的性质和复杂性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN>）一项特定控制（单独或连同其他控制）是否以及如何防止<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>或发现并纠正重大错报。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>70</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．如果在设计和实施进一步审计程序时拟利用被审计单位内部</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">生成的信息，针对该信息完整性和准确性的控制可能与审计相关。如</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">果与经营和合规目标相关的控制与注册会计师实施审计程序时评价</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">或使用的数据相关，则这些控制也可能与审计相关。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>71</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．用以防止未经授权购买、使用或处臵资产的内部控制，可能</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">包括与财务报告和经营目标相关的控制。注册会计师对这些控制的考</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">虑通常仅限于与财务报告可靠性相关的控制。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>72</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．被审计单位通常有一些与目标相关但与审计无关的控制，注</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">册会计师无需对其加以考虑。例如，被审计单位可能依靠某一复杂的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">自动化控制提高经营活动的效率和效果</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">如航空公司用于维护航班时</SPAN>间表的自动化控制系统<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>，但这些控制通常与审计无关。进一步讲，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">虽然内部控制应用于整个被审计单位或所有经营部门或业务流程，但</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">是了解与每个经营部门和业务流程相关的内部控制，可能与审计无关。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>对公共部门实体的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>73</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．对公共部门实体进行审计的注册会计师通常对内部控制负有</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">额外责任，如报告被审计单位对既定操作守则的遵守情况。注册会计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">师可能也有责任报告被审计单位对法律法规及其他监管要求的遵守</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">情况。因此，注册会计师对内部控制的评价可能更广泛、更详细。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（三）对相关控制了解的性质和程度</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>（参见本准则第十六条）<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>74</SPAN>．评价控制的设计，涉及考虑该控制单独或连同其他控制，是<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">否能够有效防止或发现并纠正重大错报。控制得到执行是指某项控制</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">存在且被审计单位正在使用。评估一项无效控制的运行没有什么意</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">义，因此需要首先考虑控制的设计。设计不当的控制可能表明存在值</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">得关注的内部控制缺陷。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>75</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．用以获取有关控制设计和执行的审计证据的风险评估程序可能包括：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）询问被审计单位人员；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）观察特定控制的运用；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）检查文件和报告；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">追踪交易在财务报告信息系统中的处理过程</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">穿行测试</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">但是，询问本身并不足以实现这些目标。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>76</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．除非存在某些可以使控制得到一贯运行的自动化控制，否则</SPAN>注册会计师对控制的了解并不足以测试控制运行的有效性。例如，某<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">一人工控制在某一时点得到执行的审计证据，并不能提供该控制在所</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">审计期间内的其他时点也有效运行的证据。但是，由于信息技术处理</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">流程的内在一贯性</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">见本指南第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>63</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">段</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">，实施审计程序确定某项自动</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">化控制是否得到执行，也可以实现对控制运行有效性测试的目标，这取决于注册会计师对控制（如针对程序变更的控制</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">）</SPAN>的评估和测试。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1231</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">针对评估的重大错报风险</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">采取的应对措施》及其应用指南对控制运行有效性的测试作出了规定</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">并提供了指引。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（四）内部控制要素</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>——</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>控制环境</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>（参见本准则第十七条）<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>77</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．控制环境包括治理职能和管理职能，以及治理层和管理层对</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">内部控制及其重要性的态度、认识和行动。控制环境设定了被审计单</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">位的内部控制基调，影响员工的内部控制意识。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>78</SPAN>．在了解控制环境时，与控制环境相关的要素可能包括下列方面：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">对诚信和道德价值观的沟通与落实，这是影响控制的设计、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">执行和监督有效性的重要因素；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）对胜任能力的重视，包括管理层对特定工作胜任能力的考虑以及这些能力如何转化为必要的技能和知识；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）治理层的参与，与这方面相关的因素举例如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US>①</SPAN>治理层相对于管理层的独立性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US>②</SPAN>治理层的经验与品德；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN 
lang=EN-US>③</SPAN>治理层参与被审计单位经营的程度和收到的信息及其对经营活动的详细检查；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN 
lang=EN-US>④</SPAN>治理层采取措施的适当性，包括提出问题的难度和对问题的跟进程度，以及治理层与内部审计人员和注册会计师的互动；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）管理层的理念和经营风格，与这方面相关的因素举例如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US>①</SPAN>承担和管理经营风险的方法；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US>②</SPAN>对财务报告的态度和措施；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US>③</SPAN>对信息处理、会计职能及人员的态度；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）组织结构，即被审计单位为实现目标而计划、执行、控制及评价其活动的框架；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">职权与责任的分配，包括如何分配经营活动的职权与责任，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">如何建立报告关系和职权等级；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN>）人力资源政策与实务，包括与招聘、培训、考核、咨询、晋升、薪酬和补救措施等相关的政策与实务。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">与控制环境要素相关的审计证据</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>79</SPAN>．通过将询问和其他风险评估程序相结合（如通过观察或检查<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>文件证实询问<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>，注册会计师可以获取相关审计证据。例如，通过询<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">问管理层和员工，注册会计师可以了解管理层如何向员工传达商业行</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">为惯例和道德行为价值观念。注册会计师可以通过考虑管理层是否建</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">立了书面行为守则以及管理层是否按照支持该守则的方式行事，来确</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">定相关控制是否已得到执行。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>80</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: 0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">对于内部审计就识别出的与审计相关的内部控制缺陷提出</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">的问题及建议，注册会计师还可能考虑管理层是如何予以回应的，包</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">括这些回应是否以及如何得以执行，内部审计是否对此进行了后续评价。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">控制环境对重大错报风险评估的影响</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>81</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．控制环境的某些要素对重大错报风险评估具有广泛影响。例</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">如，被审计单位的控制意识在很大程度上受治理层影响，因为治理层</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">的职责之一就是平衡管理层面临的与财务报告相关、源于市场需求或</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">薪酬方案的压力。与治理层参与相关的控制环境的设计有效性受下列</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">事项的影响：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）治理层相对于管理层的独立性及评价管理层措施的能力；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）治理层是否了解被审计单位从事的交易；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）治理层对财务报表是否按照适用的财务报告编制基础编制<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（包括财务报表的披露是否充分）进行评价的程度。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>82</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．活跃而独立的董事会可能影响高级管理人员的理念和经营风</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">格，其他因素对高级管理人员的影响可能有限。例如，人力资源政策</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">和实务规定招聘具有胜任能力的财务、会计和信息系统人员，这可能</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">降低处理财务信息时出现错误的风险，但是却不能抵消最高管理层高</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">估收益的强烈倾向。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>83</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．当注册会计师评估重大错报风险时，存在令人满意的控制环</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">境是一个积极的因素。虽然令人满意的控制环境有助于降低舞弊风</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">险，但并不能绝对遏制舞弊。相反，控制环境中存在的缺陷</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">特别是</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">与舞弊相关的缺陷</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">可能削弱控制的有效性。例如，管理层没有针对</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">信息系统安全风险投入足够资源，而是允许对系统程序或数据作出不</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">当修改，或允许处理未经授权的交易，这可能对内部控制产生不利影</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.05pt">响。如《〈中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1231</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">针对评估的重大错</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">报风险采取的应对措施〉应用指南》所述，控制环境也影响进一步审</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">计程序的性质、时间安排和范围。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>84</SPAN>．控制环境本身并不能防止或发现并纠正重大错报。然而，它可能影响注册会计师对其他控制（如对控制的监督和特定控制活动的运行）有效性的评价，进而影响注册会计师对重大错报风险的评估。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>85</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">．小型被审计单位的控制环境通常与较大型被审计单位的不</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt">同。例如，小型被审计单位的治理层可能不包括独立的或外部的成员，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">如果没有其他所有者，治理层的职能通常直接由业主兼经理承担。控</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">制环境的性质也可能影响其他控制的重要性或缺乏这些控制所造成</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">的后果。例如，在小型被审计单位，业主兼经理的积极参与可能抵消</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">由于缺乏职责分离导致的特定风险，但也会增加其他风险，如凌驾于</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">控制之上的风险。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>86</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">．在小型被审计单位，可能无法获取以文件形式存在的有关控</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">制环境要素的审计证据，特别是在管理层与其他人员的沟通不够正式</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.95pt">但却有效的情况下。例如，小型被审计单位可能没有书面的行为守则，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">但却通过口头沟通和管理层的示范作用形成了强调诚信和道德行为</SPAN>重要性的文化。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>87</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">．因此，管理层或业主兼经理的态度、认识和措施对注册会计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">师了解小型被审计单位的控制环境非常重要。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（五）内部控制要素<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>——</SPAN>被审计单位的风险评估过程（参见本准则第十八条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>88</SPAN>．被审计单位的风险评估过程为管理层确定需要管理的风险提供了基础。如果这一过程对于具体情况（包括被审计单位的性质、规模和复杂程度）是适当的，则有助于注册会计师识别重大错报风险。被审计单位的风险评估过程对于具体情况是否适当属于职业判断。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第二十条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>89</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．小型被审计单位可能没有正式的风险评估过程。在这种情况</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt">下，管理层很可能通过直接亲自参与经营来识别风险。无论情况如何，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">注册会计师询问识别出的风险以及管理层如何应对这些风险，仍是必要的。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体>（六）内部控制要素<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>——</SPAN>与财务报告相关的信息系统（包括相关业务流程）与沟通<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 25.9pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-width: 99%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">与财务报告相关的信息系统</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-width: 99%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-width: 99%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">包括相关业务流程</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -6.85pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-width: 99%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">第二十一条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>90</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．与财务报告目标相关的信息系统</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">包括会计系统</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">）</SPAN>由一系列<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">的程序和记录组成。被审计单位设计和建立这些程序和记录旨在：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">生成、记录、处理和报告交易</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">以及事项和情况</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">，以及为</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">相关资产、负债和所有者权益明确受托责任；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）解决不正确处理交易的问题，如自动生成暂记账户文件，以及及时按照程序清理暂记项目；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）处理并解释凌驾于控制之上或规避控制的情况；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）将信息从交易处理系统过入总分类账；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">针对除交易以外的事项和情况获取与财务报告相关的信息，如资产的折旧和摊销、应收账款可回收性的改变等；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>）确保适用的财务报告编制基础规定披露的信息得到收集、记录、处理和汇总，并在财务报表中进行了适当报告。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 29.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">财务报表可能包含从总账和明细账之外的其他途径获取的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">信息。这些信息可能包括：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）财务报表披露的从租赁协议中获取的信息，如续租选择权或未来的租赁付款额；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）财务报表披露的由被审计单位风险管理系统生成的信息；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）由管理层的专家提供并在财务报表中披露的公允价值信息；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）财务报表中披露的、从为形成财务报表确认或披露的估计所用模型或其他计算中获取的信息，包括与模型所用基础数据和假设<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">相关的信息，例如：可能影响资产使用寿命的内部假设，或不受被审</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">计单位控制的因素影响的数据</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">如利率</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）财务报表中披露的、与源于财务模型的敏感性分析相关的信息，用以表明管理层已考虑替代假设；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>）财务报表确认或披露的从被审计单位纳税申报表和记录中获取的信息；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN>）财务报表中披露的、从用于支持管理层评估被审计单位持<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">续经营能力所作分析中获取的信息，例如，与识别出的、可能导致对</SPAN>被审计单位持续经营能力产生重大疑虑的事项或情况相关的披露（如有<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 29.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">按照本准则第二十一条的要求了解与财务报告相关的信息</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">系统</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">包括了解信息系统中与财务报表所披露信息相关的信息，无论</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">这些信息是从总账和明细账中获取，还是从总账和明细账之外的其他</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">途径获取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">需要注册会计师运用职业判断。例如，被审计单位财务报</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">表中的特定金额或披露</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">如关于信用风险、流动性风险和市场风险的披露</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -5.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">可能以从被审计单位风险管理系统中获取的信息为基础。但是，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">注册会计师不需要了解风险管理系统的所有方面，而是运用职业判断</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">确定需要了解哪些方面。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>会计分录<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>93</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．被审计单位的信息系统通常包括使用标准会计分录记录重复</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">发生的交易。例如，在总分类账中记录销售、采购和现金付款，或记</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">录管理层定期作出的会计估计，如对无法收回的应收账款的估计的改变。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>94</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">．被审计单位的财务报告过程还包括使用非标准的会计分录，</SPAN>以记录不重复发生的、异常的交易或调整事项，包括合并调整、业务合并或处臵，或非重复发生的估计（如资产减值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>。在人工系统的总<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">分类账中，注册会计师可以通过检查分类账、日记账和支持性记录来</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">识别非标准的会计分录。但是，当运用自动化程序记录总分类账和编</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">制财务报表时，这些分录可能只以电子形式存在，因此使用计算机辅</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">助审计技术更易于识别。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>相关业务流程<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>95</SPAN>．被审计单位的业务流程是指旨在实现下列目的的活动：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）开发、采购、生产、销售、配送产品和提供服务；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）确保遵守法律法规；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）记录信息，包括会计和财务报告信息。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.4pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">业务流程产生的交易由信息系统记录、处理和报告。了解被审计</SPAN>单位的业务流程（包括交易产生的方式<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>，有助于注册会计师以适合<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">被审计单位具体情况的方式了解与财务报告相关的信息系统。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>96</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">．在小型被审计单位，与财务报告相关的信息系统和相关业务</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.5pt">流程</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">包括信息系统中与财务报表所披露信息相关的信息，无论这些</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">信息是从总账和明细账中获取，还是从总账和明细账之外的其他途径获取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">可能不如较大型被审计单位复杂，但其作用同样重要。管理层</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">积极参与经营管理的小型被审计单位，可能不需要详细描述会计流</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">程、复杂的会计记录或书面政策。因此，在对小型被审计单位进行审计时，了解其与财务报告相关的信息系统就较为容易，也更依赖于询</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">问而不是对文件的检查。但是，了解与财务报告相关的信息系统和相</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">关业务流程仍然重要。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">沟通</B>（参见本准则第二十二条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>97</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．被审计单位就财务报告的角色与职责以及与财务报告相关的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">重大事项的沟通，涉及到使员工了解在财务报告内部控制方面各自的角色和职责。这包括使员工了解其在财务报告信息系统中的活动与其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">他员工工作的联系的程度，以及向适当的更高层级的管理层报告例外</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">事项的方式。沟通可以采用政策手册、财务报告手册等形式。公开的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">沟通渠道有助于确保例外事项得到报告并有应对措施。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>98</SPAN>．由于职责层级较少，更容易接触到管理层，小型被审计单位<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">的沟通可能比大型被审计单位更简单、更容易实现。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（七）内部控制要素</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>——</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>控制活动</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>（参见本准则第二十三条）<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>99</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．控制活动是指有助于确保管理层的指令得以执行的政策和程</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">序。控制活动</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（不管存在于信息系统还是人工系统中</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">具有各种不同</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">的目标，运用于各种不同的组织和职能层级中。控制活动包括与下列</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">相关的活动：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）授权；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）业绩评价；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）信息处理；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）实物控制；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）职责分离。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>100</SPAN>．与审计相关的控制活动包括：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）与特别风险相关的控制活动，以及与仅通过实质性程序无<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">法获取充分、适当的审计证据的风险相关的控制活动</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">参见本准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">三十二条和第三十三条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.05pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）注册会计师运用职业判断认为相关的控制活动。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>101</SPAN>．注册会计师判断一项控制活动是否与审计相关，受以下两个因素的影响：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）注册会计师识别出的可能导致重大错报的风险；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）在确定实质性程序的范围时，注册会计师认为测试控制运行的有效性是否适当。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>102</SPAN>．注册会计师的工作重点是识别和了解重大错报风险更高的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">领域的控制活动。如果多项控制活动能够实现同一目标，注册会计师</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">不必了解与该目标相关的每项控制活动。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>103</SPAN>．除了应对账户余额和交易相关风险的控制之外，与审计相<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>关的控制活动还可能包括管理层建立的、用于应对没有按照适用的财<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">务报告编制基础进行披露导致的重大错报风险的控制。这些控制活动</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">可能与财务报表包含的从总账和明细账之外的其他途径获取的信息相关。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>104</SPAN>．注册会计师通过了解内部控制其他要素获取的关于控制活<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">动是否存在的信息，有助于其确定是否有必要对控制活动进行更多的了解。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>105</SPAN>．小型被审计单位控制活动依据的理念与较大型被审计单位<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">可能相似，但是它们运行的正式程度可能不同。进一步讲，在小型被</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">审计单位中，由于某些控制活动由管理层执行，特定类型的控制活动可能变得并不相关。例如，只有管理层拥有批准赊销、重大采购的权</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">力，这可以对重要账户余额和交易实施有力控制，降低或消除实施更</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">具体的控制活动的必要性。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>106</SPAN>．与小型被审计单位审计相关的控制活动可能与主要交易循环（如收入、采购和薪酬）相关。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">信息技术导致的风险</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第二十四条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>107</SPAN>．信息技术的采用影响被审计单位执行控制活动的方式。从<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">注册会计师的角度看，如果针对信息系统的控制能够保证系统所处理</SPAN>信息和数据的完整性和安全性，则控制是有效的。针对信息系统的控<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">制包括信息技术一般控制和应用控制。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>108</SPAN>．信息技术一般控制是与多个程序相关且支持应用控制有效<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">运行的政策或程序，应用于主机、小型机和终端用户环境。保证信息</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">完整性和数据安全性的信息技术一般控制通常包括：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）数据中心和网络运行控制；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）系统软件的购臵、修改及维护控制；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）程序修改控制；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）接触或访问权限控制；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）应用系统的购臵、开发及维护控制。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>这些控制通常用于应对本指南第<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>64</SPAN>段列示的风险。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>109</SPAN>．应用控制通常是指在业务流程层面运行的人工或自动化程<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">序，运用于由单个程序处理的交易。从性质上讲，应用控制可以是预</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">防性的或检查性的，旨在保证会计记录的完整性。因此，应用控制与</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">用于生成、记录、处理、报告交易或其他财务数据的程序相关。这些控制有助于保证发生的交易经过授权，并得到全面而准确地记录和处</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">理。应用控制的举例包括对输入数据的编辑性检查，序号检查和报告</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">例外事项的人工跟进，以及在数据录入时进行纠正。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（八）内部控制要素<SPAN lang=EN-US>——</SPAN>对控制的监督（参见本准则第二十五条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>110</SPAN>．对控制的监督是指被审计单位评价内部控制在一段时间内<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">运行有效性的过程。对控制的监督涉及及时评估控制的有效性并采取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">必要的补救措施。管理层通过持续的监督活动、单独的评价活动或两</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">者相结合实现对控制的监督。持续的监督活动通常贯穿于被审计单位</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">日常重复的活动中，包括常规管理和监督工作。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>111</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">．管理层的监督活动可能包括利用与外部有关各方沟通所获</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.3pt">取的信息</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">如可能表明存在问题或需要改进的领域的顾客投诉和监管</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">机构的意见</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>112</SPAN>．管理层对控制的监督经常通过管理层或业主兼经理对经营<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">活动的密切参与来实现。通过密切参与经营活动，可以识别出与预期</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">不同的重大差异和不准确的财务数据，从而可以对控制采取补救措施。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">被审计单位的内部审计</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第二十六条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>113</SPAN>．如果被审计单位设有内部审计，获取对内部审计的了解有助于注册会计师了解被审计单位及其环境<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN>包括内部控制<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.05pt">）</SPAN>，特别是<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">了解内部审计在</SPAN>被审计单位对财务报告内部控制的监督中的作用。这一了解，连同注册会计师按照本<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">准则第九条第一款的规定通过询问获</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">取的信息，也可能为注册会计师识别和评估重大错报风险提供直接相</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">关的信息。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>114</SPAN>．内部审计的目标和范围、职责性质及其在被审计单位中的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.8pt">地位</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">包括权威性和问责机制</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">有较大差别，取决于被审计单位的规</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">模、组织结构以及管理层和治理层</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN>如适用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">的要求。内部审计章程</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">或职权范围可能对这些事项作出规定。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>115</SPAN>．内部审计的职责可能包括实施程序并评价结果，就风险管<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">理、内部控制及治理过程的设计和有效性，向管理层和治理层提供保证。此时，内部审计可能在被审计单位对财务报告内部控制的监督中</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">发挥重要作用。然而，内部审计的职责也可能专注于评价运营的经济</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">性、效率和效果，此时，内部审计的工作可能与被审计单位的财务报</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">告并不直接相关。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 30.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN
