style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: 0.65pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">按照本准则第九条第一款的规定询问适当的内部审计人</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">员，有助于注册会计师了解内部审计的职责性质。如果认为内部审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">的职责与被审计单位的财务报告相关，注册会计师可能复核内部审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">相关期间的审计计划</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">如有</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -4.7pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">，并与适当的内部审计人员讨论该计划，</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>以进一步了解内部审计已执行或拟执行的活动。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">如果内部审计的职责性质和鉴证活动与被审计单位的财务</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">报告相关，注册会计师也可能利用内部审计的工作，以修改注册会计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">师为获取审计证据而直接实施的审计程序的性质、时间安排，或缩小</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">其范围。如果基于以前年度的审计经验或注册会计师实施的风险评估</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">程序，相对于被审计单位的规模和运营性质而言，内部审计的配备看</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">上去充分、适当，并与治理层有直接的报告关系，则注册会计师更有</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">可能利用被审计单位内部审计的工作。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">如果基于对被审计单位内部审计的初步了解，注册会计师</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">预期利用内部审计的工作，以修改拟实施的审计程序的性质、时间安</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">排，或缩小其范围，则《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>1411</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">利</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">用内部审计人员的工作》适用。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">如《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>1411</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">利用内部审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">人员的工作》所述，内部审计的活动不同于可能与财务报告相关的其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">他监督控制活动</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">例如，复核被审计单位用于防止或发现错报的管理</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">会计信息</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -7pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">在审计业务的早期与适当的内部审计人员建立沟通，并在</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">审计业务执行过程中保持这种沟通，有利于信息的有效共享。这种做</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">法能够创造一种氛围，使得注册会计师能够获悉内部审计注意到的可</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">能影响注册会计师工作的重大事项。《中国注册会计师审计准则第<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 25.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1101</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>注册会计师的总体目标和审计工作的基本要求》讨论了<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">注册会计师在计划和执行审计工作时保持职业怀疑的重要性，包括对</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">引起对作为审计证据的文件记录和对询问的答复的可靠性产生怀疑</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt">的信息保持警觉。因此，在审计业务执行过程中与内部审计保持沟通，</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">可以为内部审计人员将这些信息告知注册会计师提供机会。注册会计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">师因而能够在识别和评估重大错报风险时考虑这些信息。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">信息来源</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第二十七条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>121</SPAN>．监督活动中使用的很多信息可能由被审计单位的信息系统<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">产生。如果管理层假定用于监督的数据是准确的而这一假定没有依</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">据，则这些信息可能存在错误，导致管理层从监督活动中得出不正确</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">的结论。因此，注册会计师需要了解以下事项，并将其作为了解被审</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">计单位监督活动</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">内部控制要素</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">的一部分：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）与被审计单位监督活动相关的信息来源；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）管理层认为信息对于信息的使用目的足够可靠的依据。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><FONT 
size=3>四、识别和评估重大错报风险<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（一</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LETTER-SPACING: -2.8pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>）</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>评估财务报表层次重大错报风险</SPAN></B><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">参见本准则第二十八条第（一）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">项）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>122</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．财务报表层次重大错报风险是指与财务报表整体广泛相关，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">并潜在地影响多项认定的风险。这种性质的风险不一定限定于某类交</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">易、账户余额或披露层次的特定认定的风险，而在一定程度上代表了</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">可能增加认定层次重大错报风险的情况，如管理层凌驾于内部控制之上。财务报表层次的风险可能与注册会计师考虑由于舞弊导致的重大</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">错报风险尤其相关。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>123</SPAN>．财务报表层次的风险很可能源于控制环境存在缺陷（虽然这些风险还可能与其他因素相关，如经济下滑<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。例如，管理层缺乏<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">胜任能力或缺乏对财务报表编制过程的监督等缺陷可能对财务报表</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">具有更广泛的影响，可能需要注册会计师采取总体应对措施。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>124</SPAN>．注册会计师在了解被审计单位内部控制后，可能对被审计<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>单位财务报表的可审计性产生怀疑。例如：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）对管理层的诚信产生严重疑虑，以致注册会计师认为管理层在财务报表中作出虚假陈述的风险非常大而无法进行审计；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）对被审计单位会计记录的状况和可靠性的疑虑，可能使注<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">册会计师认为可能很难获取充分、适当的审计证据，以支持对财务报</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">表发表无保留意见。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">．《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>150</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">在审计报告中发</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">表非无保留意见》及其应用指南为注册会计师确定是否有必要出具保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">留意见、无法表示意见或在某些情况下解除业务约定</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">在适用的法律</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">法规允许解除约定的情况下</SPAN>）<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">作出了规定并提供了指引。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（二）评估认定层次重大错报风险</SPAN></B><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第二十八条第</SPAN><FONT 
size=3>（二）项）<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>126</SPAN>．注册会计师需要考虑各类交易、账户余额和披露认定层次<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">的重大错报风险，因为这些考虑直接有助于确定用于获取充分、适当</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">的审计证据而在认定层次实施的进一步审计程序的性质、时间安排和范围。在识别和评估认定层次重大错报风险时，注册会计师可能认为</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">识别出的风险与财务报表整体广泛相关，进而潜在地影响多项认定。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>对认定的运用<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>127</SPAN>．在声明财务报表按照适用的财务报告编制基础编制时，管<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">理层对各类交易和事项、账户余额以及披露的确认、计量和列报作出</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">明确或隐含的认定。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>128</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．注册会计师可以使用本指南第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>129</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">段第一项和第二项描述</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">的认定，或在能够涵盖本指南第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>129</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">段所有方面的前提下作出不同表</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">述。例如，注册会计师可能选择将关于各类交易、事项及相关披露的</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>认定与关于账户余额及相关披露的认定结合使用。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">关于各类交易、账户余额及相关披露的认定</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>129</SPAN>．注册会计师在考虑可能发生的潜在错报的不同类型时运用的认定，可以分为以下两类：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）关于所审计期间各类交易、事项及相关披露的认定：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 25.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">①</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">发生</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">记录或披露的交易和事项已发生，且这些交易和事项</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">与被审计单位有关；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 25.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">②</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">完整性</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>所有应当记录的交易和事项均已记录，所有应当包<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">括在财务报表中的相关披露均已包括；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US>③</SPAN>准确性</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>与交易和事项有关的金额及其他数据已恰当记录，相关披露已得到恰当计量和描述；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US>④</SPAN>截止</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>交易和事项已记录于正确的会计期间；<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US>⑤</SPAN>分类</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>交易和事项已记录于恰当的账户；<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 25.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">⑥</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">列报</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">交易和事项已被恰当地汇总或分解且表述清楚，相关</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">披露在适用的财务报告编制基础下是相关的、可理解的。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）关于期末账户余额及相关披露的认定：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US>①</SPAN>存在</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>记录的资产、负债和所有者权益是存在的；<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 25.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">②</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">权利和义务</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>记录的资产由被审计单位拥有或控制，记录的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">负债是被审计单位应当履行的偿还义务；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US>③</SPAN>完整性</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>所有应当记录的资产、负债和所有者权益均已记录，所有应当包括在财务报表中的相关披露均已包括；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.4pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">④</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">准确性、计价和分摊</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">资产、负债和所有者权益以恰当的金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">额包括在财务报表中，与之相关的计价或分摊调整已恰当记录，相关</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">披露已得到恰当计量和描述；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US>⑤</SPAN>分类</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>资产、负债和所有者权益已记录于恰当的账户；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 25.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">⑥</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">列报</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">资产、负债和所有者权益已被恰当地汇总或分解且表</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.95pt">述清楚，相关披露在适用的财务报告编制基础下是相关的、可理解的。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">关于其他披露的认定</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>130</SPAN>．对与记录的各类交易、事项或账户余额并非直接相关的披<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">露，注册会计师在考虑可能发生的潜在错报的不同类型时，也可能运</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.95pt">用本指南第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>129</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">段第一项和第二项描述的认定</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">可适当调整</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">。例如，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">可能要求被审计单位描述金融工具导致的风险敞口</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（包括风险是如何产生的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">；风险管理的目标、政策及流程；计量风险的方法等。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>对公共部门实体的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>131</SPAN>．当管理层对公共部门实体的财务报表作出认定时，除本指<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.05pt">南第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>129</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">段提及的认定外，管理层通常声明交易和事项已按照法律法</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">规或其他监管要求执行。这些认定可以纳入财务报表审计的范畴。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（三</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LETTER-SPACING: -4.2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>）</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>识别重大错报风险的过程</SPAN></B><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">参见本准则第二十九条第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">一）</SPAN><FONT 
size=3>项）<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>132</SPAN>．通过实施风险评估程序收集的信息，包括在评价控制的设<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">计及确定其是否得到执行时获取的审计证据，可以作为支持风险评估</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">结果的审计证据。风险评估结果决定了拟实施的进一步审计程序的性</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">质、时间安排和范围。在识别财务报表中存在的重大错报风险时，注</SPAN>册会计师按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第<SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1101</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">注册会计师</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">的总体目标和审计工作的基本要求》的规定运用职业怀疑。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>133</SPAN>．本指南附录<SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>列示了可能表明存在重大错报风险（包括与披露相关的重大错报风险）的情况和事项。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>134</SPAN>．按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第<SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1221</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>计划和执行<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">审计工作时的重要性》的要求，识别并评估各类交易、账户余额及披</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">露中存在的重大错报风险时需要考虑重要性和审计风险。注册会计师</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">对重要性的确定属于职业判断，受到注册会计师关于财务报表使用者</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">对财务报告需求的认识的影响。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>135</SPAN>．识别风险时，注册会计师对财务报表披露的考虑包括定量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">披露和定性披露，披露中可能存在重大错报</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">即如果合理预期错报可</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">能影响财务报表使用者依据财务报表整体作出的经济决策，则该错报通常被认为是重大的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。根据被审计单位及业务的具体情况，可能与<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">重大错报风险评估相关的定性披露举例如下：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）处于财务困境中的被审计单位的流动性和债务合同；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）导致确认减值损失的事项或情况；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）估计不确定性的关键来源，包括关于未来的假设；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）会计政策变更及适用的财务报告编制基础要求的其他相关<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">披露的性质，例如，财务报告的新要求预期将对被审计单位的财务状</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">况和经营成果产生重大影响；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）股份支付协议，包括如何确定应确认的金额的信息及其他相关披露；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>）关联方及关联方交易；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN>）敏感性分析，包括被审计单位估值技术中用到的假设发生<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">变化产生的影响，以使使用者能够理解记录或披露的金额背后的计量</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">不确定性。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>136</SPAN>．小型被审计单位财务报表中的披露可能细节较少或不太复<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">杂</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">例如，某些财务报告编制基础允许小型被审计单位在财务报表中</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>提供较少的披露<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。但是，这并不能减轻注册会计师了解被审计单位<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">及其环境</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">包括内部控制）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">的责任</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">在其与披露相关时</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（四</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LETTER-SPACING: -3.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>）</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>将控制与认定相联系</SPAN></B><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第二十九条第（三</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -3.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">项</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>137</SPAN>．在进行风险评估时，注册会计师可能识别出可以防止或发<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">现并纠正特定认定的重大错报的控制。一般而言，了解这些控制，并</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">在控制所在的流程和系统中将这些控制与认定相联系，是很有帮助</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">的，因为单个控制活动本身往往并不足以应对风险。通常只有多个控</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">制活动，连同内部控制的其他要素，才能足以应对风险。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>138</SPAN>．相反地，某些控制活动可能对特定类别的交易或账户余额所包含的个别认定具有特定影响。例如，被审计单位建立的用以确保<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">员工能够适当地盘点和记录年度实物存货的控制活动，与存货账户余</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">额的存在和完整性认定直接相关。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>139</SPAN>．控制可能与某一认定直接相关，也可能与某一认定间接相<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">关。关系越间接，控制在防止或发现并纠正该认定中错报的有效性越</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">小。例如，销售经理对分地区的销售网点的销售汇总情况进行复核，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">与销售收入完整性的认定只是间接相关。相应地，该项控制在降低销</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">售收入完整性认定中的错报风险方面的效果，要比与该认定直接相关的控制</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（例如，将发货单与开具的销售发票相核对）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">的效果差。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>重大错报<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>140</SPAN>．单一财务报表及披露中的潜在错报可能因其规模、性质或<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">具体情况而被认为是重大的。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（参见本准则第二十九条第</SPAN>（四）<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">项</SPAN>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（五）特别风险<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">识别特别风险</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第三十一条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>141</SPAN>．特别风险通常与重大的非常规交易和判断事项有关。非常<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">规交易是指由于金额或性质异常而不经常发生的交易。判断事项可能包括作出的会计估计（具有计量的重大不确定性</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>。经过系统处理的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">日常、简单的交易不太可能产生特别风险。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>142</SPAN>．对由于如下事项导致的重大非常规交易，重大错报风险可能更高：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）管理层更多地干预会计处理；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）对数据的收集和处理进行更多的人工干预；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）复杂的计算或会计政策；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）非常规交易的性质可能使被审计单位难以对由此产生的风险实施有效控制。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>143</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．对由于如下事项导致的需要作出会计估计的重大判断事项，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">重大错报风险可能更高：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）对涉及会计估计、收入确认等方面的会计政策存在不同的理解；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）所要求的判断可能是主观或复杂的，或需要对未来事项的影响作出假设，如对公允价值的判断。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">．《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>123</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">针对评估的重大</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">错报风险采取的应对措施》说明了识别特别风险对进一步审计程序的影响。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">与由于舞弊导致的重大错报风险相关的特别风险</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">．《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>41</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">财务报表审计中</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">与舞弊相关的责任》对识别和评估由于舞弊导致的重大错报风险作出</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">了规定。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">了解与特别风险相关的控制</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第三十二条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>146</SPAN>．虽然与重大非常规交易或判断事项相关的风险通常很少受<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">到日常控制的约束，管理层可能采取其他措施应对此类风险。相应地，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">注册会计师在了解被审计单位是否设计和执行了针对非常规交易或</SPAN>判断事项导致的特别风险的控制时，通常了解管理层是否以及如何应<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">对这些风险。管理层采取的应对措施可能包括：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）控制活动，如高级管理人员或专家对假设进行检查；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）对估计流程作出记录；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）治理层作出批准。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>147</SPAN>．如果发生诸如收到重大诉讼事项的通知等一次性事件，注<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">册会计师在考虑被审计单位的应对措施时，关注的事项包括：被审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">单位是否已将这类事项提交适当的专家</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">如内部或外部的法律顾问</SPAN>）<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">处理，是否已对该事项的潜在影响作出评估，如何建议将该情况在财</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">务报表中进行披露。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>148</SPAN>．在某些情况下，管理层可能未能通过实施针对特别风险的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">控制恰当应对特别风险。管理层未能实施这些控制表明存在值得关注</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">的内部控制缺陷。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（六）仅实施实质性程序不能获取充分、适当的审计证据的风险（参见本准则第三十三条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>149</SPAN>．重大错报风险可能与记录日常交易或账户余额以及编制可<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">靠的财务报表直接相关。这些风险可能包括对日常和重大类别的交易</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">如被审计单位的收入、采购、现金收入或现金支出</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">处理不准确或</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">不完整的风险。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>150</SPAN>．如果日常交易由高度自动化处理，不存在或存在很少人工<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">干预，针对风险仅实施实质性程序可能不可行。例如，如果被审计单</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">位大量信息在一体化的系统中仅以电子方式生成、记录、处理或报告，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">注册会计师可能认为会出现以上情况。在这种情况下：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）获取的审计证据可能仅以电子形式存在，其充分性和适当性通常取决于针对准确性和完整性的控制的有效性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）如果适当的控制没有正在有效运行，信息不当生成或对信息进行不当修改而没有被发现的可能性会增加。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">．《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>123</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">针对评估的重大</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">错报风险采取的应对措施》说明了识别出这些风险对进一步审计程序的影响。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（七）对风险评估的修正</SPAN></B><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>（参见本准则第三十四条）<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>152</SPAN>．在审计过程中，注册会计师可能注意到某些信息，其明显<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">不同于风险评估所依据的信息。例如，风险评估可能基于预期特定控</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">制运行有效这一判断，但在测试控制运行的有效性时，注册会计师获</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">取的证据可能表明这些控制在被审计期间的相关时点并未有效运行。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">类似地，在实施实质性程序时，注册会计师可能发现错报的金额或频率高于在风险评估时预计的金额或频率。在这种情况下，风险评估可能没有恰当地反映被审计单位的真实状况，原计划的进一步审计程序</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.8pt">对于发现重大错报可能无效。《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1231</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">针对评估的重大错报风险采取的应对措施》及其应用指南对此作</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">出了进一步规定并提供了进一步指引。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">五、审计工作底稿</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体>（参见本准则第三十五条）<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>153</SPAN>．注册会计师需要运用职业判断，确定对本准则第三十五条规定的事项进行记录的方式。例如，在小型被审计单位的审计中，这<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">些事项的工作底稿可能包含在总体审计策略和具体审计计划的工作</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">底稿中。类似地，风险评估的结果可以单独予以记录，也可作为注册</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">会计师对进一步审计程序记录的一部分。审计工作底稿的形式和范围</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">受被审计单位性质、规模、复杂程度、内部控制、被审计单位信息的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">可获得性，以及审计过程中使用的审计方法和技术的影响。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>154</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．对于与财务报告相关的业务和流程不太复杂的被审计单位，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">审计工作底稿可以形式简单，内容相对概括。注册会计师没有必要记</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">录对被审计单位及相关事项了解的所有内容。注册会计师记录的了解</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">的关键要素包括在重大错报风险评估时所依据的内容。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>155</SPAN>．记录的范围也能反映审计项目组成员的经验与胜任能力。<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">只要能够满足《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1131</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">审计工作底</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">稿》的要求，由经验较少的成员组成的项目组执行审计时，可能需要</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">比成员经验较多的项目组作出更加详细的记录，以帮助经验较少的成</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">员恰当了解被审计单位。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>156</SPAN>．对于连续审计，某些工作底稿在必要时可能需要结转、更新，以反映被审计单位业务或流程的变化。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">附录</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>（参见本准则第二条、第十七条至第二十七条、本指南第<SPAN 
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>77</SPAN>段至第<SPAN 
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>121</SPAN>段）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">内部控制要素</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">．本准则第二条、第十七条至第二十七条、本指南第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>77</SPAN>段至第<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>121</SPAN>段列示的内部控制要素与财务报表审计相关，本附录作出进一步说明。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><FONT size=3>一、控制环境<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>．控制环境包括以下要素：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）对诚信和道德价值观的沟通与落实。控制的有效性受负责<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">创建、管理和监控内部控制的人员的诚信和道德价值观的影响。被审</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">计单位的道德行为规范，以及这些规范如何在被审计单位内部得到沟</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">通和落实，决定了是否能产生诚信和道德的行为。例如，对诚信和道</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">德价值观的落实包括管理层采取措施消除或减少可能导致员工不诚</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">实、不守法或不道德行为的动机或诱因。被审计单位对诚信和道德价</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">值观方面政策的沟通包括通过政策规定、行为规范和示范向员工沟通</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">行为准则。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）对胜任能力的重视。胜任能力是指具备完成某一职位的工作所应有的知识和技能。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）治理层的参与程度。被审计单位的控制意识在很大程度上<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">受治理层的影响。治理层职责的重要性在被审计单位的行为守则、其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">他法律法规或在为治理层制定的指引中予以规定。治理层的职责还包</SPAN>括监督以下程序的设计和有效执行：内部举报不恰当行为的程序和用于复核内部控制有效性的程序。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）管理层的理念和经营风格。管理层的理念和经营风格具有<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">广泛的特点。例如，管理层对财务报告的态度及行为，可以通过其选</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">择保守还是激进的会计原则以及作出会计估计时的谨慎和保守态度</SPAN>得到体现。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）组织结构。建立相关的组织结构包括考虑职权和责任的关<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">键领域，以及适当的报告层级。被审计单位组织结构是否恰当部分取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">决于被审计单位的规模和经营活动的性质。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>）职权与责任的分配。职权与责任的分配可能包括与适当的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">经营惯例、关键员工的知识和经验、履行职责时提供的资源相关的政</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">策。此外，还可能包括一些政策及交流活动，用于保证所有员工均了</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">解被审计单位目标、相互之间的工作联系以及个人的工作对实现目标</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">的作用，认识到如何以及对什么承担责任。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN>）人力资源政策与实务。人力资源政策与实务通常能显示与被审计单位控制意识相关的重要事项。例如，如果招聘录用标准要求<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">录用最胜任的员工</SPAN>（即强调教育背景、以前的工作经验、以前取得的成就、诚信和道德行为的证明<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>，则表明被审计单位希望录用有胜任<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">能力并值得信赖的人员。被审计单位的培训政策可以传达预期角色及</SPAN>职责，并包括实务性培训<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">（</SPAN>如培训学校和研讨会<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>，这表明了员工预<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">期的工作表现和行为方式。通过定期业绩考核予以晋升的政策表明被</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">审计单位希望具备相应资格的员工承担更高级别的职责。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><FONT 
size=3>二、被审计单位的风险评估过程<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>．就财务报告的目的而言，被审计单位的风险评估过程包括管理层如何识别与按照适用的财务报告编制基础编制财务报表相关的<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">经营风险，估计其重要性，评估其发生的可能性，针对这些风险采取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">措施应对和管理风险及其结果。例如，被审计单位的风险评估过程可</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">能针对被审计单位如何考虑交易未被记录的可能性，或识别并分析财</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">务报表中记录的重大估计。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>．与可靠的财务报告相关的风险包括可能发生的外部和内部事<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt">项、交易或情况，这些事项、交易或情况会对被审计单位生成、记录、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">处理和报告财务报表中与管理层认定相一致的财务数据产生不利影</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">响。管理层可能会制定计划、执行程序或采取措施以解决特定风险，</SPAN>或者出于成本或其他考虑决定接受风险。以下情况可能会产生或改变风险：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）监管环境和经营环境的变化。监管环境和经营环境的变化会导致竞争压力的变化以及显著不同的风险。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）新员工。新员工可能对内部控制有不同的关注点或认识。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）新的或升级的信息系统。信息系统重大、快速的变化会改变与内部控制有关的风险。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）快速增长。重要、快速的业务扩张可能使控制难以应对，从而增加了控制失效的风险。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）新技术。将新技术运用于生产过程或信息系统可能改变与内部控制相关的风险。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>）新业务模式、产品或活动。进入新的业务领域和发生新的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">交易，可能因被审计单位具有较少的经验而带来新的与内部控制相关的风险。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN>）公司重组。重组可能带来裁员和监督及职责分离的变化，可能改变与内部控制相关的风险。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>）扩张海外经营。在海外扩张或收购海外企业会产生新的并<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">且往往是独特的风险，进而可能影响内部控制，如由于外币交易产生</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">的额外或已变化的风险。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN>）新的会计政策。采用新的会计政策或变更会计政策可能影响财务报表编制过程中的风险。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><FONT 
size=3>三、与财务报告相关的信息系统（包括相关业务流程）与沟通<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">．信息系统包括基础设施</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">实物或硬件部分</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">、软件、人员、程</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">序及数据。很多信息系统都广泛使用信息技术。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>．与财务报告目标相关的信息系统（包括财务报告系统）包括关于下列事项的方法和记录：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）识别与记录所有的有效交易；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）以充分详细的方式及时地描述交易，以便在财务报告中对交易作出恰当分类；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）以在财务报表中正确记录交易的货币价值的方式计量交易的价值；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）确定交易发生的期间，以便将交易计入恰当的会计期间；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）在财务报表中对交易及相关披露作出恰当反映。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN>．信息系统生成信息的质量，影响管理层在管理和控制被审计单位活动时作出恰当的决策以及编制可靠的财务报告的能力。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>．沟通，涉及使员工了解各自在财务报告内部控制方面的角色<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt">和职责，可以采用政策手册、会计和财务报告手册以及备忘录等形式。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">沟通也可以采用电子方式或口头方式，以及通过管理层的行动来实</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">现。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><FONT size=3>四、控制活动<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN>．通常情况下，可能与审计相关的控制活动可以分为与下列事项相关的政策和程序：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）业绩评价。这些控制活动包括被审计单位分析及评价实际<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">业绩与预算、预测和前期业绩的差异，将不同类别的数据</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">经营或财务数据</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">）</SPAN>联系起来，分析之间的关系，进行调查并采取纠正措施；将<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">内部数据与外部信息相比较；评价职能部门、项目活动的业绩。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）信息处理。信息系统控制活动的两大类是应用控制和信息<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">技术一般控制。应用控制运用于处理单个应用程序，信息技术一般控</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">制是与多个应用程序相关的政策和程序，通过保证信息系统持续恰当</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">地运行，支持应用控制作用的有效发挥。应用控制的举例包括对记录</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.15pt">计算准确性的检查，对账户和试算平衡表的维护和审核，自动控制</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN>如设臵对输入数据和数字序号的自动检查<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>，以及对例外报告的人工跟<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">进调查。信息技术一般控制的举例包括程序变动控制，限制接触程序</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">或数据的控制，对实施新发布的软件包应用程序的控制，针对限制接触或监督使用系统应用程序的系统软件的控制，使用这些系统应用程</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">序可能更改财务数据或记录而不留下审计轨迹。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）实物控制。实物控制包括下列控制：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN 
lang=EN-US>①</SPAN>保证资产的实物安全，包括恰当的安全保护措施，如针对接触资产和记录的安全设施；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US>②</SPAN>对接触计算机程序和数据文档设臵授权；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.4pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">③</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">定期</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">盘点并将盘点记录与控制记录相核对（如将会计记录与现金、有价证券和存货的定期盘点结果相比较）。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">旨在防止资产盗窃的实物控制，与财务报表编制的可靠性及审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">相关，相关的程度取决于资产被侵占的风险。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）职责分离。即将交易授权、记录交易以及资产保管等职责<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">分配给不同员工。职责分离旨在降低同一员工在正常履行职责过程中</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">实施并隐瞒舞弊或错误的可能性。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">．某些控制活动可能取决于是否存在由管理层或治理层制定</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">的、恰当的高层次政策。例如，可能按照既定的指导方针</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">如治理层</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">制定的投资标准</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.35pt">）</SPAN>进行授权控制；或者，非常规交易<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">如重大收购或撤资</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -5.9pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">可能需要特定的高级别的批准，包括在某些情况下由股东批准。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><FONT size=3>五、对控制的监督<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.4pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>11</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．管理层的一项重要职责就是持续不断地建立和维护控制。管</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">理层对控制的监督包括考虑控制是否按计划运行，以及控制是否根据</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">情况的变化作出恰当修改。例如，对控制的监督可能包括管理层对是</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">否及时编制银行存款余额调节表进行复核，内部审计人员评价销售人</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">员是否遵守被审计单位关于销售合同条款的政策，法律部门监控被审</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">计单位的道德规范和商业行为政策是否得到遵守等。监督也用于保证</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">控制持续有效运行。例如，如果没有对编制银行存款余额调节表的及</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">时性和准确性进行监督，相关人员可能停止编制该表。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．内部审计人员或具有类似职责的人员可以通过单独评价促成</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">对被审计单位控制的监督。他们通常定期提供关于内部控制职能的信</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">息</SPAN>（着力于评价内部控制的有效性<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -6.9pt">）</SPAN>，就内部控制的优势和缺陷进行<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">沟通，并提出改进建议。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 19.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>13</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．监督活动可能包括利用与外部有关机构或人员沟通所获取的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">信息，这些外部信息可能显示内部控制存在的问题或需要改进的领</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">域。例如，客户通过付款来间接表示其同意发票金额，或者对发票金</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">额提出异议。此外，监管机构可能会对影响内部控制运行的问题与被</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>审计单位沟通（例如，银行监管机构针对检查所作的沟通<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。在执行<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">监督活动时，管理层也可能考虑与注册会计师就内部控制进行沟通。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">附录</SPAN><FONT 
face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>（参见本指南第<SPAN 
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>41</SPAN>段和第<SPAN 
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>133</SPAN>段）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">可能表明存在重大错报风险的情况和事项</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">以下是可能表明财务报表存在重大错报风险的情况和事项的示</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">例。这些情况和事项涵盖范围广泛，然而，并非所有的情况和事项都</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">与每项审计业务相关，下面所列情况和事项也不一定完整。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>．在经济不稳定（如货币发生重大贬值或经济发生严重通货膨胀）的国家或地区开展业务；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 25.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">．在高度波动的市场开展业务</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">如期货交易</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>．在高度复杂的监管环境中开展业务；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>．持续经营和资产流动性出现问题，包括重要客户流失；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle
