style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>．获取资本或借款的能力受到限制；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>．被审计单位经营所处的行业发生变化；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN>．供应链发生变化；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>．开发新产品或提供新服务，或进入新的业务领域；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN>．开辟新的经营场所；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>10</SPAN>．被审计单位发生变化，如发生重大收购、重组或其他异常的事项；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>11</SPAN>．拟出售分支机构或业务分部；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN>．存在复杂的联营或合资企业；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>13</SPAN>．运用表外融资、特殊目的实体以及其他复杂的融资安排；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>14</SPAN>．从事重大的关联方交易；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>15</SPAN>．缺乏具备会计和财务报告技能的员工；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">．关键人员变动</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">包括核心执行人员的离职</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>17</SPAN>．内部控制存在缺陷，尤其是管理层未处理的内部控制缺陷；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>18</SPAN>．管理层和员工编制虚假财务报告的动机；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>19</SPAN>．信息技术战略与经营战略不协调；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN>．信息技术环境发生变化；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>21</SPAN>．安装新的与财务报告有关的重大信息技术系统；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>22</SPAN>．经营活动或财务业绩受到监管机构或政府机构的调查；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt">．以往发生的错报或错误，或者在本期期末出现重大会计调整；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>24</SPAN>．发生大额非常规或非系统性交易（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">包括公司间的交易和在期</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">末发生大量收入的交易</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>25</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．按照管理层特定意图记录的交易</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">如债务重组、资产出售和</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">交易性债券的分类</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>26</SPAN>．采用新的会计准则；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>27</SPAN>．涉及复杂过程的会计计量；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>28</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．涉及重大计量不确定性</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">包括会计估计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">的事项或交易及相</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">关披露；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>29.</SPAN>遗漏披露应包含的重大信息或信息晦涩难懂；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8CxSpLast 
style="MARGIN: auto 7.35pt auto 0cm; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>30</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．存在未决诉讼和或有负债</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">如售后质量保证、财务担保和环</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">境补救</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
